# Diagram: research/orchestrator/tasks/transforms/ground_counts_task.py


> Auto-generated by Obscura crawlers

## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([GroundCountsTask.run]) --> GetOutput[Get output path]
    GetOutput --> CallSparkMain[Call spark_main]
    CallSparkMain --> CreateSpark[Create Databricks Spark session]
    CreateSpark --> ExecuteQuery[Execute SQL query]
    ExecuteQuery --> ConvertPandas[Convert to Pandas DataFrame]
    ConvertPandas --> ConnectRedis[Connect to Redis db=11]
    ConnectRedis --> CreatePipeline[Create Redis pipeline]
    CreatePipeline --> GetMaxDate[Get most recent date]
    GetMaxDate --> LoopStart{For each row}
    LoopStart --> CheckBatch{Batch size >= 500?}
    CheckBatch -->|Yes| ExecutePipe[Execute pipeline]
    ExecutePipe --> ResetCounter[Reset counter]
    ResetCounter --> BuildKey[Build location+date key]
    CheckBatch -->|No| BuildKey
    BuildKey --> SetHash[HSET metrics]
    SetHash --> SetExpire[EXPIRE 1 week]
    SetExpire --> IncrementCounter[Increment counter]
    IncrementCounter --> CheckRecent{Is most recent date?}
    CheckRecent -->|Yes| BuildRecentKey[Build location-only key]
    BuildRecentKey --> SetRecentHash[HSET metrics]
    SetRecentHash --> SetRecentExpire[EXPIRE 1 week]
    SetRecentExpire --> IncrementAgain[Increment counter]
    IncrementAgain --> LoopStart
    CheckRecent -->|No| LoopStart
    LoopStart -->|Done| FinalCheck{Counter > 0?}
    FinalCheck -->|Yes| FinalExecute[Execute pipeline]
    FinalCheck -->|No| WriteFile[Write 'Done' to output]
    FinalExecute --> WriteFile
    WriteFile --> End([Complete])
```

```mermaid
    GroundCountsTask ..> DatabricksSession : uses
    GroundCountsTask ..> Redis : uses
    GroundCountsTask ..> luigi : framework
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Luigi
    participant GroundCountsTask
    participant spark_main
    participant Databricks
    participant Redis
    
    Luigi->>GroundCountsTask: run()
    GroundCountsTask->>GroundCountsTask: output().path
    GroundCountsTask->>spark_main: spark_main(output_path)
    spark_main->>Databricks: Create session
    Databricks-->>spark_main: session
    spark_main->>Databricks: Execute QUERY
    Databricks-->>spark_main: DataFrame
    spark_main->>spark_main: toPandas()
    spark_main->>Redis: Connect(host, port, db=11)
    Redis-->>spark_main: connection
    spark_main->>Redis: pipeline()
    loop For each row
        spark_main->>spark_main: Check batch size
        alt Batch full
            spark_main->>Redis: execute()
        end
        spark_main->>Redis: hset(location+date key, metrics)
        spark_main->>Redis: expire(key, 1 week)
        alt Is most recent date
            spark_main->>Redis: hset(location key, metrics)
            spark_main->>Redis: expire(key, 1 week)
        end
    end
    spark_main->>Redis: execute() final
    spark_main->>spark_main: Write 'Done' file
    spark_main-->>GroundCountsTask: complete
    GroundCountsTask-->>Luigi: task complete
```
